✥﹤┈┈┈┈   ┈┈┈┈﹥✥
2000-2001

Pimple packs, metal cases, small and large format DVD style cases are all common packing types during version 6.0. The free trial hours was raised to 700 intially and then to 1000 by the end of this version run. Many of the discs during this period are rebranded earlier discs with 6.0 installtion media; many others would be recycled in future releases.
Version 6.0
Software Date 10/04/00
Free Hours 700
Format CD-ROM

Packaging Metal Case With Lid
Packaging Variants Tall Format Case
